 Contrary to the Chinese government's assertion that Jawaharlal Nehru accepted the 1890 treaty between China and the British in relation to Sikkim in support of China's claim over the Doklam region, the former prime minister told China that he was the chief of Bhutan's territory Is claiming on the part
 nehru ne apane chini samakaksh chau en laai ko 26 sitambar, 1959 ko bheje gaye apane patr main kaha tha, 'aapke is bayaan kaa thik-thik prabhaav hamen spasht nahin he ki sikkim or bhutan kii seemaa maujuuda charchaa ke daayre main nahin aati he
 In this letter PTI received in Beijing, Nehru said, "in fact, the Chinese map shows a large part of Bhutan as part of Tibet
" ' seemaa vivaad par bharat ke rukh ko ujagar karte hue lambey-chaude patr main nehru ne likhaa tha ki bhutan ke saath sandhi ke tahat bhutan ke bahari sambandhon ke sambandh main anya sarkaron ke saath maamalon ko uthaane ke liye ekmaatr sakasham praadhikaar bharat sarkaar he or usne bhutan sarkaar kii taraf se kai maamle china ke samaksh uthaae hai
 He wrote, 'such is the case of the correction of the error in the Chinese map in relation to the border of Bhutan with Tibet, which is to be discussed along the border of India with the Tibet region of China in the same region
 ' chini maanchitr main bhutan ke bade hisse ko china ke hisse ke taur par darshaae jane kii baat par jor dene ke baad nehru ne 1890 ke china or angrejon ke bich hue samjhaute kaa ullekh kiya tha, jiske jariye sikkim par bharat kii samprabhutaa manjuur kii gai thi
 Nehru had said, 'regarding Sikkim, the Chinese government only in 1890 believed that the internal administration and foreign relations of that state had direct and exclusive control by the Government of India
 is 1890 kii sandhi ne sikkim or tibet ke bich seemaa ko bhi paribhaashit kiya or baad main 1895 main seemaa kaa simakan hua
 Therefore, there is no dispute about the border of Sikkim with the Tibet region
 'tippaniyan He also said, 'it is wrong to say that the frontier of Bhutan as shown in the Chinese map is the traditional frontier
 iske vipareet, yah macmahon rekha he jo is kshetra main paaramparik seemaa kaa sahi pratinidhitiv karti he
 The water divide created by the Himalayan peaks is a natural frontier, which has been accepted by people on both sides as a border for centuries

 ye paramparaon ke khilaaf he

 bataa den ki anand karaj hindu dharm ke vivaah se bilkul alag mana jaataa he
 This ritual takes place during the day
 paaramparik hindu shaadiyon main lagn, muhoort, janmpatriyon kaa milaanaa jaruri hota he
 These rituals do not hold much importance in Anand Karaj
 sikh dharm main jo log guru par puri aasthaa rakhte hai, ve anand karaj karte hai
 Every day is sacred to them
 bollywood main inhen apana best friend maanati hai sonam kapooranand karaj main granthi gurugranth sahib kaa paath karte hai
 During this time, all families have a turban or a sarapa on their head
 ye rasm pheron se pehle hoti he
 Journalism means mass communication has changed over time
 nai-nai takneekon ke kaaran ab patrakarita ke kai plateform dekhne ko mil rahe hai
 After print, radio and TV, the future of journalism has come on the web
 agar aap kii dilchaspisamachar, duniya main ghat rahi ghatnaon or likhane main he to aap is field main aa sakate hai
 To make career in journalism, 12th pass from any stream is necessary
 12veen ke baad aap chahen to diploma, certificate yaa degree course kar sakate hai
 Many major colleges in India teach mass media at degree level
 agar aap grajuation ke baadapatrkaritaaki padhai karnaa chaahate hai to yah aapke liye zyada phydemand hogi
 After graduation, PG Diploma in Mass Communication, Diploma in Public Relations can be done
 vahiin, sidhe do varshiya piji degree bhi hasil kar sakate hai

phil directly

 Print journalism opportunities are available in many languages of the country
 print main mukhya rup se megsine, akhbaar ke liye kaam kar sakate hai
 Electronic Journalism: Electronic Journalism brought journalism from the world of letters to the world of visuals
 audio, video, tivi, radio ke madhyam se yah dur-daraaj ke kshetra main bhi lokapriy hone laga
 It has become the largest platform for journalism through TV satellite, cable service and new technologies
 web patrakarita:patrakarita ke is plateform ne reader, visitors ko feedback kii suvidha di, yani aap news mekar se sidhe sawaal puch sakate hai
 With the arrival of smart phones, it is increasing every day
 patrakarita ke bhavishya ke rup main is madhyam ko sthapit kiya ja rahaa he
 Public relations: This field is a little different from journalism, it is also taught during the study of journalism
 kisi vyakti, santhaan kii chhavi ko logon kii najar main sakaaratmak rup se prastut karnaa public relation main aata he
 After taking a course in public relations, work is done for business houses, political persons, celebrities and institutions
 jaruri yogyata:jarnalism ke field menkarirbanane ke liye sabase zyada jaruri he aapkaa maansik rup se majboot hona yani kisi bhi paristhiti main khud par vishwaas karke kaam par dhyaan dena
 At the same time, to be a journalist, keeping yourself updated with news with the best communication skills is the biggest rule of journalism
 aapke vichaaron main nishpakshta honi chahie, koi bhi cheez kehane se pehle aapke paas uske pruf hone chahie
 Your thinking is like an analyst on any subject, it is most important
 kya karnaa hoga aapako:patrkaar ke rup main aapako field or desk donon par kaam karnaa pad saktaa he
 Field work consists of the work of a reporter and research department
 field work ke kaam main ve log zyada acha kar sakate hai jinhen socity kii samaj he or sampark sutara achche hen
 The main job of a reporter is to go to a press conference, interview, gather information about an event
 agar aapaki dilchaspee photography main he to aapako field main cameraman kaa kaam mil saktaa he
 The job of a cameraman is not just to take photographs but to bring such photos which can be found with the news
 vahiin, desk par news riting, editing kaa kaam miltaa he
 For this, you must have language knowledge
 naukari ke avasar:patrakarita kii padhai karne ke baad aapako news agency, news website, production house, privet or sarkari news channel, prasar bharti, publication dizin, film mekking main rojgaar se avasar milte hai
 You can also do freelancing if you want

 Today, in the changing scenario, humans have become not only more curious but also aware
 jansanchaar ke anekanek madhyam aaj hamaare saamne hai
 The 24-hour news channel is also at the forefront of this
 kisi bhi ghatana ke byore ko samvedansheel tareeke se logon tak pahunchane kii jimmedaari in channelon kii hi he

 jiske baad ye panel apni report supreme court ko degaa
 Read about how the matter will be resolved after the Supreme Court's decision on Friday
 
 
 1
 ramjanmabhoomi-babri Masjid was sent by the Supreme Court for arbitration, for which the name of 3 arbitrators has been fixed
 2
 Spiritual Guru Sri Sri Ravi Shankar, retired Supreme Court Justice Ibrahim Khalifullah, Senior Advocate Shri Ram Panchu are included in this panel
 3
 This panel will have to begin its hearing within a week
 4
 The entire hearing of the arbitration of ramjanmabhoomi-babri Masjid dispute will be held in Faizabad
 5
 The panel will have to submit its report to the Supreme Court within 8 weeks, although in the meantime the panel will continuously submit the status report to the court
 6
 The state government will have to make all arrangements for the hearing in Faizabad
 7
 During the arbitration, there is a ban on print media and TV media, that is, the entire process will not be reported
